I create images and architectural visualizations. <br/><br/>
Founder of One Visual Design in 2013, while working professionally I have been involved in many computer graphic projects of the highest caliber. I am a great team player and passionate about improving my craft through continual training with new technology and design principles. I also pride myself on being highly organized and working efficiently in demanding environments that require flexibility.<br/><br/>
